Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-401 Short title.
------------------------------------------
This part is known as the "Utah Percent-for-Art Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-402 Purpose.
--------------------------------------
This part is designed to:Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-402(1): 9-6-410 establish a program which administers that portion of appropriations for capital expenditures which is set aside:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-402(1)(a): for the acquisition of works of art used for public buildings; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-402(1)(b): 9-6-410 to facilitate public art installations as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-402(2): enhance the quality of life in the state by placing art of the highest quality in public spaces where it is seen by the general public;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-402(3): promote and preserve appreciation for and exposure to the arts; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-402(4): foster cultural development in the state and encourage the creativity and talents of its artists and craftspeople.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403 Definitions.
------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(1): "Artist" means a practitioner in the visual arts, generally recognized by critics and the artist's peers as a professional who is committed to producing high quality work on a regular basis, and who is not the project architect or a member of the project's architectural firm.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(2): "Acquired or constructed" means acquired, constructed, reconstructed, restored, enlarged, improved, renovated, repaired, replaced, equipped, or furnished in whole or in part with state funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(3): "Contracting agency" means the state agency which is responsible for supervising the principal user of a state building or facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(4): "Public art installation" means a work of art:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(4)(a): owned by a:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(4)(a)(i): county of the first class; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(4)(a)(ii): municipality or metro township in a county of the first class;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(4)(b): created by an artist, with a preference for a Utah artist;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(4)(c): located in a public place where the county of the first class, municipality in a county of the first class, or metro township in a county of the first class has jurisdiction; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(4)(d): that is intended to be a permanent fixture in the public place.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(5): "Principal user" means the department, board, commission, institution, or agency of the state for the principal use of which a state building or facility is acquired or constructed.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(6): 9-6-410
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(6)(a): "Program" means the Percent-for-Art Program created in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(6)(b): 9-6-410 "Program" does not mean the Public Art Installation Initiative created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(7): "Project" means the project whereby state buildings or facilities are acquired or constructed.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(8)(a): "State building or facility" means a state building, permanent structure, facility, park, or appurtenant structure thereof, wholly or partially enclosed, which includes, but is not restricted to a space or facility used or to be used for carrying out the functions of a department, board, commission, institution, or agency of the state, including offices, hearing or meeting rooms, auditoriums, libraries, courtrooms, classrooms, workshops, laboratories, eating or sleeping facilities, or highway rest areas.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(8)(b): "State building or facility" does not include motor pools, heating plants, sheds, sewers, parking lots, bridges, highways, or buildings used solely for storage or warehousing.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(9): "Utah artist" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(9)(a): an individual who produces paintings, drawings, photos, sculptures, or similar works; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(9)(b): who has:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(9)(b)(i): lived in Utah a minimum of ten years; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(9)(b)(ii): a primary residence in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-403(10): "Work of art" or "works of art" means any form of original creation of visual art including, but not restricted to any sculpture, bas relief, high relief, mobile, fountain, painting, graphic, print, lithograph, etching, embossing, drawing, mural, mosaic, supergraphic, fresco, photograph, ceramic, fiber, mixed media, or combination of forms.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404 Creation of program -- Use of appropriations.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(1): A Percent-for-Art Program shall be administered by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2): 63A-5b-609; 63A-5b-609; 9-6-410
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2)(a): 63A-5b-609
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2)(a)(i): 63A-5b-609 Before January 1, 2035, an appropriation received by or available to the director under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2)(a)(ii): Beginning January 1, 2035, any appropriation received by or available to the director shall be used to acquire existing works of art or to commission the creation of works of art placed in or at appropriate state buildings or facilities as determined by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2)(b): 63A-5b-609; 9-6-410 For appropriations annually received by or available to the director under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2)(b)(i): eighty percent shall be used to acquire existing works of art or to commission the creation of works of art placed in or at appropriate state buildings or facilities as determined by the division; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2)(b)(ii): 9-6-410 twenty percent shall be used to support the Public Art Installation Initiative described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-404(2)(c): Any unexpended funds remaining at the end of the fiscal year shall be nonlapsing and not revert to the General Fund.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405 Procedures, guidelines, and rules.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1): The division shall follow these guidelines in administering the program:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(a): Works of art shall be acquired under the program for use only with respect to those buildings or facilities that the division determines have significant public use or access, especially where the design and technical construction of the building or facility lend themselves to works of art.  All funds set aside and administered by the program from appropriations for any state building or facility of which any part is obtained from the issuance of bonds shall be used only to acquire works of art that will be placed in or at, and remain a part of, that building or facility, to the extent necessary to preserve the federal income tax exemption otherwise allowed for interest paid on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(b): The goal of the division in administering the program is to fairly distribute works of art throughout the various social, economic, and geographic communities of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(c): The division:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(c)(i): shall give first preference to Utah artists; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(c)(ii): may consider artists from other states and give preference to artists from other states that have similar percent-for-art programs and demonstrate a reciprocal preference for Utah artists.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(d): The division shall involve the director of the Division of Facilities Construction and Management, or the director's designee, and the project architect in the process of screening or selecting works of art or artists to create works of art for each project and shall involve in that process representatives from the project's principal user or contracting agency, the community in which the project is located, and the art profession.  The project's principal user or contracting agency shall have representation at least equal to any other entity on the selection committee, as designated by the project's president or director.  Any selection and placement of art shall be by a majority decision of the user agency representatives on the committee and a majority decision of the entire committee.  The selection and placement shall be approved by the president or director of the principal user.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(e): Any relocation of art placed under this program shall be done with the participation from the division and the Division of Facilities Construction and Management and with approval from the president or director of the principal user.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(1)(f): The costs of administering the program and conserving and maintaining all works of art placed under the program are limited to 15% of the funds deposited in the Utah Percent-for-Art Account.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-405(2): The division shall adopt procedures, guidelines, and rules as necessary to implement this chapter and administer the program.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-406 Director to enter into contracts.
---------------------------------------------------------------
The director may enter into contracts on behalf of the division to acquire works of art and to commission artists for the creation of works of art as selected by the division or committees established by the division, and may sue and be sued in the name of the division upon these contracts.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-407 Title to work of art vests in the name of the state -- Title subject to restrictions and interests.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-407(1): Title to a work of art acquired by or created for the program vests upon its completion, installation, and final acceptance in the division in the name of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-407(2): Title to a work of art acquired from appropriations for any state building or facility of which any part is obtained from the issuance of bonds, and placed in or at that building or facility, is subject to the same restrictions and interests as title to that building or facility, to the extent necessary to preserve the federal income tax exemption otherwise allowed for interest paid on those bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-408 Division responsible for maintenance and security.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The division is responsible, in cooperation with the contracting agency, for the conservation, maintenance, and security of all works of art placed in or at each state building or facility under the program.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409 Rights of artist commissioned by program.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
An artist who is commissioned by the program to create a work of art has the following rights with respect to that work of art:Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409(1): all rights secured to the artist under federal copyright laws;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409(2): the right to claim authorship of the work of art;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409(3): the right to photographic reproduction of the work of art;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409(4): the right of first refusal:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409(4)(a): to conduct all repair and conservation work on the work of art in accordance with accepted principles of professional conservation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409(4)(b): to purchase the work of art if the state decides to sell it; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-409(5): the right to deny further association of the artist's name with or authorship of the work of art if conservation or repair work is done by a person other than the artist, which in the opinion of the artist damages its integrity.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410 Public Art Installation Initiative.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1)(a): "Applicant" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1)(a)(i): a county of the first class;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1)(a)(ii): a municipality in a county of the first class; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1)(a)(iii): a metro township in a county of the first class.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1)(b)(i): "Local funds" means money in the possession of a county, municipality, or metro township through local revenue generation, private donation, or federal or philanthropic grant.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(1)(b)(ii): "Local funds" does not mean money from a state grant.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(2): There is created a Public Art Installation Initiative to be administered by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(3): Within available funds, the division may award an applicant a dollar-for-dollar match on the purchase or commission of a public art installation as described in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(4): Before the division may offer a dollar-for-dollar match as described in Subsection (3), an applicant shall provide the division with:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(4)(a): documentation of the local funds dedicated to the proposed public art installation;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(4)(b): a description or rendering of the proposed public art installation;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(4)(c): a copy of any contractual agreement the applicant has with the proposed artist, or a template contractual agreement to be offered to an artist; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(4)(d): any other information requested by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(5): 9-6-402 The division shall establish by rule in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(5)(a): an application process;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(5)(b): 9-6-402 a process to approve or deny an application, in accordance with the purposes described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(5)(c): a process to prioritize applications in the event of limited funding.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(6): The division:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(6)(a): may solicit and receive a donation to further the objectives of this section; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(6)(b): shall deposit any donation received to further the objectives of this section and reserve the use of that donation for the Public Art Installation Initiative.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-410(7): 9-6-404 A donation under Subsection (6) may not supplant appropriations for the Public Art Installation Initiative as described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-501 Definitions.
------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-501(1): "Endowment fund" means any endowment fund created under this chapter by a qualifying organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-501(2): "Qualifying organization" means any Utah nonprofit arts or museum organization that qualifies under this chapter to create an endowment fund, receive state money into the endowment fund, match state money deposited into the endowment fund, and expend interest earned on the endowment fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-501(3): 9-6-502 "State fund" means the Utah Arts and Museums Endowment Fund created in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-502 Utah Arts and Museums Endowment Fund.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-502(1): There is created an expendable special revenue fund known as the "Utah Arts and Museums Endowment Fund."
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-502(2): The state fund shall be administered by the division in accordance with applicable law.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-502(3): Any administrative costs incurred by the division shall be reviewed by the appropriate appropriations committee of the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-502(4): The state fund shall contain all money appropriated to the state fund by the Legislature, all federal funds received for purposes of this part, plus interest and other income earned on money in the state fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-502(5): The division shall distribute money in the state fund to qualifying arts and museum organizations to assist those organizations in creating their own arts and museums endowment funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-502(6): The division may use money in the state fund for expenses related to administering the state fund.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503 Arts and museums endowment funds.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(1): Any Utah nonprofit arts or museum organization that meets the requirements described in this part may create an endowment fund into which there may be deposited money from the state fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(2): The principal of each endowment fund described in this section may not be expended by the qualifying organization and shall be held in perpetuity solely by the qualifying organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(3): Interest income earned on the amount in each endowment fund described in this section may be expended by the qualifying organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(4): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act The principal of each endowment fund described in this section shall be invested in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(5): If a qualifying organization that creates an endowment fund as described in this section receives:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(5)(a): $50,000 or more from the state fund, the money shall be administered by the qualifying organization's professional management in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(5)(b): less than $50,000 from the state fund, the money shall be placed in a state fiduciary fund under the direction of the state treasurer, and the state treasurer shall allocate interest income to the qualifying organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-503(6): If an endowment fund is under the direction of the state treasurer, the state treasurer shall deduct administrative costs related to the endowment fund before allocating any interest income to the qualifying organization.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504 Duties of the division.
-----------------------------------------------------
The division, in accordance with the provisions of this part, shall:Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(1): 9-6-503 allocate money from the state fund to the endowment fund created by a qualifying organization under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(2): determine the eligibility of each qualifying organization to receive money from the state fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(3): determine the matching amount each qualifying organization shall raise in order to qualify to receive money from the state fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(4): establish a date by which each qualifying organization shall provide its matching funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(5): verify that matching funds have been provided by each qualifying organization by the date determined in Subsection (4); and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(6)(a): in accordance with the provisions of this part and Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act, the division may establish criteria by rule for determining the eligibility of qualifying organizations to receive money from the state fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(6)(b): in making rules under this Subsection (6), the division may consider the recommendations of the arts and museums board.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504 Duties of the division.
-----------------------------------------------------
The division, in accordance with the provisions of this part, shall:Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(1): 9-6-503 allocate money from the state fund to the endowment fund created by a qualifying organization under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(2): determine the eligibility of each qualifying organization to receive money from the state fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(3): determine the matching amount each qualifying organization shall raise in order to qualify to receive money from the state fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(4): establish a date by which each qualifying organization shall provide its matching funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(5): verify that matching funds have been provided by each qualifying organization by the date determined in Subsection (4); and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(6)(a): in accordance with the provisions of this part and Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act, the division may establish criteria by rule for determining the eligibility of qualifying organizations to receive money from the state fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-504(6)(b): in making rules under this Subsection (6), the division may consider the recommendations of the arts and museums board.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505 Eligibility requirements of qualifying arts and museum organizations -- Allocation limitations -- Matching requirements.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(1): 9-6-503 Any qualifying organization may apply to receive money from the state fund to be deposited in an endowment fund the organization has created under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(1)(a): if the qualifying organization has received a grant from the division during one of the three years immediately before making application for state fund money under this Subsection (1); or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(1)(b): upon recommendation of the arts and museums board if the qualifying organization has not received a grant from the board within the past three years.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(a): The maximum amount that may be allocated to each qualifying organization from the state fund shall be determined by the division by calculating the average cash income of the qualifying organization during the past three fiscal years as contained in the qualifying organization's final reports on file with the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(b): The division shall notify each qualifying organization of the maximum amount of money from the state fund for which the qualifying organization qualifies.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(c): The minimum amount that may be allocated to each qualifying organization from the state fund is $2,500.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(d): If the maximum amount for which the organization qualifies under the calculation described in Subsection (2)(a) is less than $2,500, the organization may still apply for $2,500.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(3)(a): After the division determines that a qualifying organization is eligible to receive money from the state fund and before any money is allocated to the qualifying organization from the state fund, the qualifying organization shall match the amount qualified for with money raised and designated exclusively for that purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(3)(b): State money, in-kind contributions, and preexisting endowment gifts may not be used to match money from the state fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4): The amount of match money described in Subsection (3) that a qualifying organization is required to provide shall be based on a sliding scale as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4)(a): any amount requested not exceeding $100,000 shall be matched one-to-one;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4)(b): any additional amount requested that makes the aggregate amount requested exceed $100,000 but not exceed $500,000 shall be matched two-to-one; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4)(c): any additional amount requested that makes the aggregate amount requested exceed $500,000 shall be matched three-to-one.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(a): Qualifying organizations shall raise the matching amount within three years after applying for money from the state fund by a date determined by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(b): Money from the state fund shall be released to the qualifying organization only upon verification by the board that the matching money has been received on or before the date determined under Subsection (5)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(c): Verification of matching funds shall be made by a certified public accountant.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(d): Money from the state fund shall be released to qualifying organizations with professional endowment management in increments not less than $20,000 as audited confirmation of matching funds is received by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(e): Money from the state fund shall be granted to each qualifying organization on the basis of the matching funds a qualifying organization has raised by the date determined under Subsection (5)(a).


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505 Eligibility requirements of qualifying arts organizations -- Allocation limitations -- Matching requirements.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(1): 9-6-503 Any qualifying organization may apply to receive money from the state fund to be deposited in an endowment fund the organization has created under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(1)(a): if the qualifying organization has received a grant from the division during one of the three years immediately before making application for state fund money under this Subsection (1); or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(1)(b): upon recommendation of the arts and museums board, if the qualifying organization has not received a grant from the board within the past three years.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(a): The maximum amount that may be allocated to each qualifying organization from the state fund shall be determined by the division by calculating the average cash income of the qualifying organization during the past three fiscal years as contained in the qualifying organization's final reports on file with the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(b): The division shall notify each qualifying organization of the maximum amount of money from the state fund for which the qualifying organization qualifies.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(c): The minimum amount that may be allocated to each qualifying organization from the state fund is $2,500.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(2)(d): If the maximum amount for which the organization qualifies under the calculation described in Subsection (2)(a) is less than $2,500, the organization may still apply for $2,500.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(3)(a): After the division determines that a qualifying organization is eligible to receive money from the state fund and before any money is allocated to the qualifying organization from the state fund, the qualifying organization shall match the amount qualified for with money raised and designated exclusively for that purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(3)(b): State money, in-kind contributions, and preexisting endowment gifts may not be used to match money from the state fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4): The amount of match money described in Subsection (3) that a qualifying organization is required to provide shall be based on a sliding scale as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4)(a): any amount requested not exceeding $100,000 shall be matched one-to-one;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4)(b): any additional amount requested that makes the aggregate amount requested exceed $100,000 but not exceed $500,000 shall be matched two-to-one; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(4)(c): any additional amount requested that makes the aggregate amount requested exceed $500,000 shall be matched three-to-one.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(a): Qualifying organizations shall raise the matching amount within three years after applying for money from the state fund by a date determined by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(b): Money from the state fund shall be released to the qualifying organization only upon verification by the board that the matching money has been received on or before the date determined under Subsection (5)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(c): Verification of matching funds shall be made by a certified public accountant.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(d): Money from the state fund shall be released to qualifying organizations with professional endowment management in increments not less than $20,000 as audited confirmation of matching funds is received by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-505(5)(e): Money from the state fund shall be granted to each qualifying organization on the basis of the matching funds a qualifying organization has raised by the date determined under Subsection (5)(a).


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-506 Unallocated money.
------------------------------------------------
Money in the state fund that is unallocated shall be reallocated by the division on a proportionate basis to qualifying organizations that raise 100% of their required match by the date determined under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-507 Spending restrictions -- Return of endowment.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-507(1): If a qualifying organization has received endowment money from the state fund, the qualifying organization may not expend any of that money or the required matching money in the qualifying organization's endowment fund, but may expend only the interest income earned on the money in the endowment fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-507(2): 9-6-506 If the division determines that a qualifying organization has expended any amount of the endowment money received from the state fund or any amount of the required matching money:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-507(2)(a): the qualifying organization shall return the amount of money the qualifying organization received from the state fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-507(2)(b): 9-6-506 the division shall reallocate any such returned money to qualifying organizations in the manner as provided in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 9-6-508 Federal match.
--------------------------------------------
The creation of the state fund and the use of state fund money to enable qualifying organizations to create endowment funds may be construed as a state match for any arts funding provided by the federal government.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 9 - Chapter 7 - Library Development
***************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101 Definitions.
------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(1): 9-7-204 "Board" means the State Library Board created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(2): 9-7-208 "Digital library" means the web-accessible digital library of state publications created under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(3): "Division" means the State Library Division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(4): 9-7-215 "Internet policy" means the public library online access policy required in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(5): "Legislative staff office" means the Office of Legislative Research and General Counsel.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(6): "Legislative publication" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(6)(a): the Utah Code after the legislative staff office prepares an updated Utah Code database incorporating amendments to the Utah Code;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(6)(b): the Laws of Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(6)(c): the Utah Constitution after the legislative staff office incorporates into the Utah Constitution amendments to the Utah Constitution that passed during the preceding regular general election.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(7): 9-7-402; 9-7-502 "Library board" means the library board of directors appointed locally as authorized by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(8): "Physical format" means a transportable medium in which analog or digital information is published, such as print, microform, magnetic disk, or optical disk.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(9): "Political subdivision" means a county, city, town, school district, public transit district, redevelopment agency, or special improvement or taxing district.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10)(a): "State agency" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10)(a)(i): the state; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10)(a)(ii): an office, department, division or other agency or instrumentality of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10)(b): "State agency" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10)(b)(i): the Office of Legislative Research and General Counsel;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10)(b)(ii): a political subdivision; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(10)(b)(iii): a state institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(11): 53B-2-101 "State institution of higher education" means an institution described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(12): 63A-16-601
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(12)(a): "State publication" means any information issued or published by a state agency for distribution.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(12)(b): "State publication" includes a book, compilation, directory, map, fact sheet, newsletter, brochure, bulletin, journal, magazine, pamphlet, periodical, report, video recording, and electronic publication.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-101(12)(c): 63A-16-601 "State publication" does not include public information, as that term is defined in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201 State Library Division -- Creation -- Purpose.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(1): There is created within the department the State Library Division under the administration and general supervision of the executive director or the designee of the executive director.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(2): The division shall be under the policy direction of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(3)(a): The division shall function as the library authority for:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(3)(a)(i): general library services;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(3)(a)(ii): mobile library services;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(3)(a)(iii): providing for permanent public access to state publications; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(3)(a)(iv): other services considered proper for a state library.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-201(3)(b): The division is responsible for providing access to legislative publications, as provided in this part, that the legislative staff office deposits with the division.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-202 Appointment of director.
------------------------------------------------------
The executive director, in consultation with the board, shall appoint a director of the division:Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-202(1): to serve as the chief administrative officer of the division; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-202(2): who has a degree from an accredited institution in library science and has demonstrated administrative ability.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203 Division duties.
----------------------------------------------
Subject to the requirements of this part, the division shall:Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(1): establish, operate, and maintain:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(1)(a): a state publications collection;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(1)(b): a digital library of state publications and legislative publications; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(1)(c): a bibliographic control system;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(2): cooperate with:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(2)(a): other state agencies to facilitate public access to government information through electronic networks or other means;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(2)(b): other state or national libraries or library agencies; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(2)(c): the federal government or agencies in accepting federal aid whether in the form of funds or otherwise;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(3): receive bequests, gifts, and endowments of money and deposit the funds with the state treasurer to be placed in the State Library Donation Fund, which funds shall be held for the purpose, if any, specifically directed by the donor; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(4): receive bequests, gifts, and endowments of property to be held, used, or disposed of, as directed by the donor:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(4)(a): in accordance with the division's policies for collection development; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-203(4)(b): with the approval of the Division of Finance.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204 State Library Board -- Members -- Meetings -- Expenses.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(1): There is created within the department the State Library Board.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(2)(a): The board shall consist of nine members appointed by the governor.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(2)(b): One member shall be appointed on recommendation from each of the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(2)(b)(i): the State Board of Education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(2)(b)(ii): the Utah System of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(2)(c): Of the seven remaining members at least two shall be appointed from rural areas.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(3): (3)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(3)(a): (3)(b) Except as required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(3)(b): The governor shall, at the time of appointment or reappointment, adjust the length of terms to ensure that the terms of board members are staggered so that approximately half of the board is appointed every two years.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(4): The members may not serve more than two full consecutive terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(5): When a vacancy occurs in the membership for any reason, the replacement shall be appointed for the unexpired term in the same manner as originally appointed.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(6): A simple majority of the members of the board constitutes a quorum for conducting board business.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(7): The governor shall select one of the board members as chair who shall serve for a period of two years.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(8): The director of the State Library Division is the executive officer of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(9): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A member may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service, but may receive per diem and travel expenses in accordance with:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(9)(a): 63A-3-106 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(9)(b): 63A-3-107 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-204(9)(c): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 rules made by the Division of Finance pursuant to Sections


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205 Duties of board and director.
-----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1): The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(a): promote, develop, and organize a state library and make provisions for the state library's housing;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(b): promote and develop library services throughout the state in cooperation with other state or municipal libraries, schools, or other agencies wherever practical;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(c): promote the establishment of district, regional, or multicounty libraries as conditions within particular areas of the state may require;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(d): supervise the books and materials of the state library and require the keeping of careful and complete records of the condition and affairs of the state library;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(e): establish policies for the administration of the division and for the control, distribution, and lending of books and materials to those libraries, institutions, groups, or individuals entitled to them under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(f): serve as the agency of the state for the administration of state or federal funds that may be appropriated to further library development within the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(g): aid and provide general advisory assistance in the development of statewide school library service and encourage contractual and cooperative relations between school and public libraries;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(h): give assistance, advice, and counsel to all tax-supported libraries within the state and to all communities or persons proposing to establish a tax-supported library and conduct courses and institutes on the approved methods of operation, selection of books, or other activities necessary to the proper administration of a library;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(i): furnish or contract for the furnishing of library or information service to state officials, state departments, or any groups that in the opinion of the director warrant the furnishing of those services, particularly through the facilities of traveling libraries to those parts of the state otherwise inadequately supplied by libraries;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(j): where sufficient need exists and if the director considers it advisable, establish and maintain special departments in the state library to provide services for the blind, visually impaired, persons with disabilities, and professional, occupational, and other groups;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(k): administer a state publications and legislative publications library program by collecting state publications and legislative publications, providing access to state publications and legislative publications through the digital library, and providing a bibliographic control system;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(l): require the collection of information and statistics necessary to the work of the state library and the distribution of findings and reports;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(m): make any report concerning the activities of the state library to the governor as the governor may require; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(1)(n): develop standards for public libraries.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-205(2): The director shall, under the policy direction of the board, carry out the responsibilities under Subsection (1).


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-206 State Library Donation Fund -- Deposits and fees.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-206(1): There is created an expendable special revenue fund entitled the "State Library Donation Fund" to receive bequests, gifts, and endowments of money.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-206(2): Any interest or proceeds realized from the use or disposition of property received by the division or interest on the fund itself shall be deposited in the State Library Donation Fund and used by the State Library Division for the purposes specified by the donor.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-206(3): All fees paid to the library and collections made due to damaged books or through sale or exchange of books and other materials shall be deposited in the General Fund as dedicated credits for use by the State Library Division.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207 Deposit of state publications and legislative publications.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(1): (1)(a); (1)(a); 46-5-108
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(1)(a): A state agency shall submit to the division a digital copy of each state publication the state agency makes available to the public regardless of format for bibliographic listing and permanent retention in the digital library.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(1)(b): (1)(a) A state agency may not remove a state publication that is posted to the state agency's public website until the state agency submits a digital copy of the state publication to the division under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(1)(c): (1)(a); 46-5-108 A state agency's submission of a state publication under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(2): (1); (2)(a); (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(2)(a): (1) In addition to the requirements of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(2)(b): (2)(a); (2)(a) The division shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(2)(b)(i): (2)(a) forward one copy of each state publication described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(2)(b)(ii): (2)(a) retain two copies of each state publication described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(3): 46-5-108
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(3)(a): Upon the legislative staff office's production of a legislative publication, the legislative staff office shall deposit with the division a digital copy of the legislative publication.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(3)(b): 46-5-108 The legislative staff office's deposit of a legislative publication with the division for the division to publish online, as provided in this part, is a method for the legislative staff office to comply with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(4)(a): A political subdivision or state institution of higher education may submit to the division a digital copy of any information the political subdivision or state institution of higher education makes available to the public.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-207(4)(b): With respect to information submitted to the division by political subdivisions and state institutions of higher education, the division may select the information the division considers appropriate for permanent public access in the digital library.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-208 Digital library for permanent public access.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-208(1): 9-7-207(1) The division shall manage and maintain an online, web-accessible digital library for state publications submitted to the division by state agencies under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-208(2): The division shall provide for permanent public access to state publications in the digital library.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-208(3): The digital library shall be accessible by agency, author, title, subject, keyword, text search, and such other means as provided by the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-208(4): The division shall make state publications in the digital library available for download.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-211 Local libraries -- Annual reports.
----------------------------------------------------------------
All municipal, city, county, and public school libraries shall submit an annual report to the director of the division on the condition and affairs of each library as required by the State Library Board.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-212 Contracts with nonpublic libraries.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
The director of the division, subject to the direction and approval of the State Library Board, may contract with nonpublic libraries to receive their library services and to otherwise coordinate the state library program with those libraries.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-213 Rulemaking.
-----------------------------------------
The division may make rules in accordance withUtah Code Annotated § 9-7-213(1): 9-7-207 standards for submitting state publications to the division under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-213(2): the method by which grants are made to individual libraries, but not including appropriations made directly to any other agency or institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-213(3): standards for the certification of public librarians; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-213(4): 9-7-215 standards for the public library online access policy required in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-214 Intentionally defacing, injuring, destroying, or refusing to return property -- Misdemeanor.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Whoever intentionally defaces, injures, or refuses to return on demand, or destroys any property belonging to the state library or loaned through its coordinating agencies or facilities, is guilty of a class B misdemeanor.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-215 Internet and online access policy required.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-215(1): 76-5b-103; 76-10-1201 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-215(1)(a): 76-5b-103 "Child sexual abuse material" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-215(1)(b): 76-10-1201 "Harmful to minors" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-215(1)(c): "Obscene" means the same as that term is defined in 20 U.S.C. Sec. 9101.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-215(1)(d): "Technology protection measure" means a technology that blocks or filters Internet access to visual depictions.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-215(2): (2)(a)(i); (2)(b)(i) State funds may not be provided to any public library that provides public access to the Internet unless the library:

Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216 Process and content standards for Internet policy.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(1)(a): Each library's Internet policy shall be developed under the direction of the library board, adopted in an open meeting, and have an effective date.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(1)(b): The library board shall review the policy at least every three years.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(1)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(1)(c)(i): Notice of the availability of the policy shall be posted in a conspicuous place within the library for all patrons to observe.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(1)(c)(ii): The library board may issue any other public notice the library board considers appropriate to inform the community about the policy.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(2): 9-7-215; 9-7-215; (1)(b) The Internet policy shall include the following information:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(2)(a): 9-7-215; 9-7-215 a statement indicating:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(2)(a)(i): 9-7-215 that the library restricts access to Internet or online sites that contain material described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(2)(a)(ii): 9-7-215 how the library board intends to meet the requirements of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(2)(b): a statement informing patrons that administrative procedures and guidelines for the staff to follow in enforcing the policy have been adopted and are available for review at the library;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(2)(c): a statement informing patrons that procedures for use by patrons and staff to handle complaints about the policy, the policy's enforcement, or about observed patron behavior have been adopted and are available for review at the library; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-216(2)(d): (1)(b) a footnote indicating the effective date of the last review of the policy under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-217 Reporting.
----------------------------------------
The division shall submit a report to the department regarding the compliance of library boards with the provisions of Sections

Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218 Criminal background check policy required -- Scope and content -- Dissemination.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(1): 9-7-402; 9-7-501 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(1)(a): "Minor" means an individual who is under 18 years old.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(1)(b): 9-7-402; 9-7-501 "Public library" means a library established under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(1)(c): "Qualifying position" means any paid or unpaid employment position with a public library, including a volunteer position, that involves significant contact with minors, as determined by the public library's library board.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(1)(d): "Qualifying prospective employee" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(1)(d)(i): is 18 years old or older; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(1)(d)(ii): applies for a qualifying position with a public library.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(2): (3) State funds may not be provided to a public library unless the public library implements a criminal background check policy that:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(2)(a): (3) meets the requirements of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(2)(b): is adopted by:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(2)(b)(i): the library board in an open meeting; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(2)(b)(ii): the county or city in which the public library is located.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3): (3)(c)(iii) The criminal background check policy shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3)(a): identify each qualifying position with the public library;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3)(b): require each qualifying prospective employee to submit to a criminal background check as a condition of employment in a qualifying position;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3)(c): establish procedures for:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3)(c)(i): gathering, submitting, and reviewing criminal background checks for qualifying prospective employees before making any offer of employment;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3)(c)(ii): disqualifying a qualifying prospective employee from employment based on information received as a result of a criminal background check; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3)(c)(iii): allowing a qualifying prospective employee to respond to information received as a result of a criminal background check;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-7-218(3)(d): (3)(c)(iii) ensure that a qualifying prospective employee who is disqualified from employment because of information obtained through a criminal background check receives:
