Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114 Computing Partnerships Grants program.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1): There is created the Computing Partnerships Grants program consisting of the grants created in this part to provide for the design and implementation of a comprehensive K-16 computing partnerships program, based upon the following common elements:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(a): outreach and student engagement;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(b): courses and content;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(c): instruction and instructional support;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(d): work-based learning opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(e): student retention;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(f): industry engagement;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(g): stacked credentials that allow for multiple exit and entry points;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(h): competency-based learning strategies; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(1)(i): secondary and post-secondary collaborations.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2): The grant program shall incentivize public schools and school districts to work with the STEM Action Center, staff of the State Board of Education, Talent Ready Utah, industry representatives, and secondary partners on the design and implementation of comprehensive K-16 computing partnerships through:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2)(a): leveraging existing resources for content, professional learning, and instruction, including existing career and technical education funds, programs, and initiatives;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2)(b): allowing for the support of professional learning for pre- and in-service educators;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2)(c): supporting activities that promote and enhance access, diversity, and equity;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2)(d): supporting collaborations and partnerships between K-12, institutions of higher education, cultural and community partners, and industry representatives;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2)(e): identifying the appropriate credentials that align with industry needs and providing the credentials in a stacked credentials pathway;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2)(f): implementing a collaborative network that enables sharing and identification of best practices; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(2)(g): providing infrastructure assistance that allows for the support of new courses and the expansion of capacity for existing courses.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(3): The grant program shall include the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(3)(a): rigorous and relevant metrics that are shared by all grant participants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(3)(b): an evaluation by the STEM Action Center of the grant program that identifies best practices.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (5) The STEM Action Center, in consultation with the State Board of Education, shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(a): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(a)(i): for the administration of the grant program and awarding of grants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(a)(ii): that define outcome-based measures appropriate to the type of grant awarded under this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(b): establish a grant application process;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(c): (5) in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(c)(i): metrics to analyze the quality of a grant application;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(c)(ii): approval of a grant application; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(c)(iii): criteria to establish a requirement for an applicant to demonstrate financial need; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(4)(d): with input from the review committee, adopt metrics to analyze the quality of a grant application.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(5)(a): The review committee shall consist of K-16 educators, staff of the State Board of Education, representatives of Talent Ready Utah, post-secondary partners, and industry representatives.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(5)(b): The review committee shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(5)(b)(i): review a grant application submitted;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(5)(b)(ii): make recommendations to a grant applicant to modify the grant application, if necessary; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(5)(b)(iii): make recommendations regarding the final disposition of an application.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-22-114(6): The STEM Action Center shall report annually on the grant program to the State Board of Education and any findings and recommendations on the grant program shall be included in the STEM Action Center annual report to the Education Interim Committee.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 9 - Chapter 23 - Pete Suazo Utah Athletic Commission Act
************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101 Definitions.
-------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(1): 76-1-101.5 "Bodily injury" has the same meaning as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(2): "Boxing" means the sport of attack and defense using the fist, which is covered by an approved boxing glove.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3): 9-23-316
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(a): 9-23-316 "Club fighting" means any contest of unarmed combat, whether admission is charged or not, where:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(a)(i): the rules of the contest are not approved by the commission;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(a)(ii): a licensed physician, osteopath, or physician assistant approved by the commission is not in attendance;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(a)(iii): a correct HIV negative test regarding each contestant has not been provided to the commission;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(a)(iv): the contest is not conducted in accordance with commission rules; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(a)(v): 9-23-316 the contestants are not matched by the weight standards established in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(b): "Club fighting" does not include sparring if:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(b)(i): it is conducted for training purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(b)(ii): no tickets are sold to spectators;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(b)(iii): no concessions are available for spectators;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(b)(iv): protective clothing, including protective headgear, a mouthguard, and a protective cup, is worn; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(3)(b)(v): for boxing, 16 ounce boxing gloves are worn.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(4): "Commission" means the Pete Suazo Utah Athletic Commission created by this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(5): "Contest" means a live match, performance, or exhibition involving two or more persons engaged in unarmed combat.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(6): "Contestant" means an individual who participates in a contest.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(7): "Designated commission member" means a member of the commission designated to:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(7)(a): attend and supervise a particular contest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(7)(b): act on the behalf of the commission at a contest venue.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(8): "Director" means the director appointed by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(9): "Elimination unarmed combat contest" means a contest where:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(9)(a): a number of contestants participate in a tournament;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(9)(b): the duration is not more than 48 hours; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(9)(c): the loser of each contest is eliminated from further competition.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(10): "Exhibition" means an engagement in which the participants show or display their skills without necessarily striving to win.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(11): "Judge" means an individual qualified by training or experience to:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(11)(a): rate the performance of contestants;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(11)(b): score a contest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(11)(c): determine with other judges whether there is a winner of the contest or whether the contestants performed equally, resulting in a draw.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12): "Licensee" means an individual licensed by the commission to act as a:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12)(a): contestant;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12)(b): judge;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12)(c): manager;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12)(d): promoter;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12)(e): referee;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12)(f): second; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(12)(g): other official established by the commission by rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(13): "Manager" means an individual who represents a contestant for the purpose of:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(13)(a): obtaining a contest for a contestant;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(13)(b): negotiating terms and conditions of the contract under which the contestant will engage in a contest; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(13)(c): arranging for a second for the contestant at a contest.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(14): "Promoter" means a person who engages in producing or staging contests and promotions.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(15): "Promotion" means a single contest or a combination of contests that:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(15)(a): occur during the same time and at the same location; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(15)(b): is produced or staged by a promoter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(16): "Purse" means any money, prize, remuneration, or any other valuable consideration a contestant receives or may receive for participation in a contest.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(17): "Referee" means an individual qualified by training or experience to act as the official attending a contest at the point of contact between contestants for the purpose of:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(17)(a): enforcing the rules relating to the contest;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(17)(b): stopping the contest in the event the health, safety, and welfare of a contestant or any other person in attendance at the contest is in jeopardy; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(17)(c): acting as a judge if so designated by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(18): "Round" means one of a number of individual time periods that, taken together, constitute a contest during which contestants are engaged in a form of unarmed combat.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(19): "Second" means an individual who attends a contestant at the site of the contest before, during, and after the contest in accordance with contest rules.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(20): 76-1-101.5 "Serious bodily injury" has the same meaning as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(21): "Total gross receipts" means the amount of the face value of all tickets sold to a particular contest plus any sums received as consideration for holding the contest at a particular location.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22): "Ultimate fighting" means a live contest, whether or not an admission fee is charged, in which:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(a): contest rules permit contestants to use a combination of boxing, kicking, wrestling, hitting, punching, or other combative contact techniques;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(b): contest rules incorporate a formalized system of combative techniques against which a contestant's performance is judged to determine the prevailing contestant;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(c): contest rules divide nonchampionship contests into three equal and specified rounds of no more than five minutes per round with a rest period of one minute between each round;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(d): contest rules divide championship contests into five equal and specified rounds of no more than five minutes per round with a rest period of one minute between each round; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(e): contest rules prohibit contestants from:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(e)(i): using anything that is not part of the human body, except for boxing gloves, to intentionally inflict serious bodily injury upon an opponent through direct contact or the expulsion of a projectile;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(e)(ii): striking a person who demonstrates an inability to protect himself from the advances of an opponent;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(e)(iii): biting; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(22)(e)(iv): direct, intentional, and forceful strikes to the eyes, groin area, Adam's apple area of the neck, and the rear area of the head and neck.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(23): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(23)(a): "Unarmed combat" means boxing or any other form of competition in which a blow is usually struck which may reasonably be expected to inflict bodily injury.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(23)(b): "Unarmed combat" does not include a competition or exhibition between participants in which the participants engage in simulated combat for entertainment purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(24): "Unlawful conduct" means organizing, promoting, or participating in a contest which involves contestants that are not licensed under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act "Unprofessional conduct" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(a): entering into a contract for a contest in bad faith;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(b): participating in any sham or fake contest;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(c): participating in a contest pursuant to a collusive understanding or agreement in which the contestant competes in or terminates the contest in a manner that is not based upon honest competition or the honest exhibition of the skill of the contestant;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(d): engaging in an act or conduct that is detrimental to a contest, including any foul or unsportsmanlike conduct in connection with a contest;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(e): failing to comply with any limitation, restriction, or condition placed on a license;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(f): striking of a downed opponent by a contestant while the contestant remains on the contestant's feet, unless the designated commission member or director has exempted the contest and each contestant from the prohibition on striking a downed opponent before the start of the contest;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(g): after entering the ring or contest area, penetrating an area within four feet of an opponent by a contestant, manager, or second before the commencement of the contest; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(25)(h): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act as further defined by rules made by the commission under
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26): "White-collar contest" means a contest conducted at a training facility where no alcohol is served in which:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a): for boxing:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a)(i): neither contestant is or has been a licensed contestant in any state or an amateur registered with USA Boxing, Inc.;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a)(ii): no cash prize, or other prize valued at greater than $35, is awarded;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a)(iii): protective clothing, including protective headgear, a mouthguard, a protective cup, and for a female contestant a chestguard, is worn;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a)(iv): 16 ounce boxing gloves are worn;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a)(v): the contest is no longer than three rounds of no longer than three minutes each;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a)(vi): no winner or loser is declared or recorded; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(a)(vii): the contestants do not compete in a cage; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b): for ultimate fighting:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(i): neither contestant is or has been a licensed contestant in any state or an amateur registered with USA Boxing, Inc.;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(ii): no cash prize, or other prize valued at greater than $35, is awarded;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(iii): protective clothing, including a protective mouthguard and a protective cup, is worn;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(iv): downward elbow strikes are not allowed;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(v): a contestant is not allowed to stand and strike a downed opponent;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(vi): a closed-hand blow to the head is not allowed while either contestant is on the ground;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(vii): the contest is no longer than three rounds of no longer than three minutes each; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-101(26)(b)(viii): no winner or loser is declared or recorded.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201 Commission -- Creation -- Appointments -- Terms -- Expenses -- Quorum.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(1): There is created within the department the Pete Suazo Utah Athletic Commission consisting of five members.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(2)(a): The governor shall appoint three commission members.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(2)(b): The president of the Senate and the speaker of the House of Representatives shall each appoint one commission member.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(2)(c): The commission members may not be licensees under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3): (3)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3)(a): (3)(b) Except as required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3)(b): The governor shall, at the time of appointment or reappointment, adjust the length of the governor's appointees' terms to ensure that the terms of members are staggered so that approximately half of the commission is appointed every two years.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3)(c): When a vacancy occurs in the membership for any reason, the replacement shall be appointed for the unexpired term.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3)(d): A commission member may be removed for any reason and replaced in accordance with this section by:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3)(d)(i): the governor, for a commission member appointed by the governor;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3)(d)(ii): the president of the Senate, for a commission member appointed by the president of the Senate; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(3)(d)(iii): the speaker of the House of Representatives, for a commission member appointed by the speaker of the House of Representatives.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(4)(a): A majority of the commission members constitutes a quorum.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(4)(b): A majority of a quorum is sufficient authority for the commission to act.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(5): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A member may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service, but may receive per diem and travel expenses in accordance with:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(5)(a): 63A-3-106 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(5)(b): 63A-3-107 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(5)(c): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 rules made by the Division of Finance under Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-201(6): The commission shall annually designate one of its members to serve as chair for a one-year period.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-202 Commission director.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-202(1): The commission shall employ a director, who may not be a member of the commission, to conduct the commission's business.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-202(2): The director serves at the pleasure of the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-203 Commission powers and duties.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-203(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The commission shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-203(1)(a): purchase and use a seal;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-203(1)(b): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act adopt rules for the administration of this chapter in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-203(1)(c): prepare all forms of contracts between sponsors, licensees, promoters, and contestants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-203(1)(d): hold hearings relating to matters under its jurisdiction, including violations of this chapter or rules made under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-203(2): The commission may subpoena witnesses, take evidence, and require the production of books, papers, documents, records, contracts, recordings, tapes, correspondence, or other information relevant to an investigation if the commission or its designee considers it necessary.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-204 Inspectors.
------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-204(1): The commission may appoint one or more official representatives to be designated as inspectors, who shall serve at the pleasure of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-204(2): Each inspector must receive from the commission a card authorizing that inspector to act as an inspector for the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-204(3): An inspector may not promote or sponsor any contest.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-204(4): Each inspector may receive a fee approved by the commission for the performance of duties under this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-205 Affiliation with other commissions.
------------------------------------------------------------------
The commission may affiliate with any other state, tribal, or national boxing commission or athletic authority.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301 Licensing.
-----------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1): A license is required for a person to act as or to represent that the person is:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1)(a): a promoter;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1)(b): a manager;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1)(c): a contestant;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1)(d): a second;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1)(e): a referee;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1)(f): a judge; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(1)(g): another official established by the commission by rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2): (1)(g) The commission shall issue to a person who qualifies under this chapter a license in the classifications of:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2)(a): promoter;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2)(b): manager;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2)(c): contestant;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2)(d): second;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2)(e): referee;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2)(f): judge; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(2)(g): (1)(g) another official who meets the requirements established by rule under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(3): 9-23-304; 9-23-307; 9-23-310; 9-23-313 All money collected under this section and Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4): 63J-1-504 Each applicant for licensure as a promoter shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(a): submit an application in a form prescribed by the commission;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(b): 63J-1-504 pay the fee determined by the commission under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(c): provide to the commission evidence of financial responsibility, which shall include financial statements and other information that the commission may reasonably require to determine that the applicant or licensee is able to competently perform as and meet the obligations of a promoter in this state;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(d): make assurances that the applicant:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(d)(i): is not engaging in illegal gambling with respect to sporting events or gambling with respect to the promotions the applicant is promoting;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(d)(ii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have engaged in or attempted to engage in any fraud or misrepresentation in connection with a contest or any other sporting event; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(d)(iii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have violated or attempted to violate any law with respect to a contest in any jurisdiction or any law, rule, or order relating to the regulation of contests in this state or any other jurisdiction;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(e): acknowledge in writing to the commission receipt, understanding, and intent to comply with this chapter and the rules made under this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(4)(f): if requested by the commission or the director, meet with the commission or the director to examine the applicant's qualifications for licensure.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5): 63J-1-504 Each applicant for licensure as a contestant shall:

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5)(c): 63J-1-504 pay the fee established by the commission under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5)(e): make assurances that the applicant:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5)(e)(i): is not engaging in illegal gambling with respect to sporting events or gambling with respect to a contest in which the applicant will participate;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5)(e)(ii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have engaged in or attempted to have engaged in any fraud or misrepresentation in connection with a contest or any other sporting event; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5)(e)(iii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have violated or attempted to violate any law with respect to contests in any jurisdiction or any law, rule, or order relating to the regulation of contests in this state or any other jurisdiction;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5)(f): acknowledge in writing to the commission receipt, understanding, and intent to comply with this chapter and the rules made under this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(5)(g): if requested by the commission or the director, meet with the commission or the director to examine the applicant's qualifications for licensure.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(6): 63J-1-504 Each applicant for licensure as a manager or second shall:

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(6)(c)(ii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have engaged in or attempted to have engaged in any fraud or misrepresentation in connection with a contest or any other sporting event; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(6)(c)(iii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have violated or attempted to violate any law with respect to a contest in any jurisdiction or any law, rule, or order relating to the regulation of contests in this state or any other jurisdiction;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(6)(d): acknowledge in writing to the commission receipt, understanding, and intent to comply with this chapter and the rules made under this chapter; and

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(7)(c)(i): is not engaging in illegal gambling with respect to sporting events or gambling with respect to a contest in which the applicant is participating;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(7)(c)(ii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have engaged in or attempted to have engaged in any fraud or misrepresentation in connection with a contest or any other sporting event; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(7)(c)(iii): has not been found in a criminal or civil proceeding to have violated or attempted to violate any law with respect to contests in any jurisdiction or any law, rule, or order relating to the regulation of contests in this state or any other jurisdiction;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(7)(d): acknowledge in writing to the commission receipt, understanding, and intent to comply with this chapter and the rules made under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(7)(e): provide evidence satisfactory to the commission that the applicant is qualified by training and experience to competently act as a referee or judge in a contest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(7)(f): if requested by the commission or the director, meet with the commission or the director to examine the applicant's qualifications for licensure.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(8): The commission may make rules concerning the requirements for a license under this chapter, that deny a license to an applicant for the violation of a crime that, in the commission's determination, would have a material affect on the integrity of a contest held under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(9): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(9)(a): A licensee serves at the pleasure, and under the direction, of the commission while participating in any way at a contest.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301(9)(b): A licensee's license may be suspended, or a fine imposed, if the licensee does not follow the commission's direction at an event or contest.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301.5 License by endorsement.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301.5(1): As used in this section, "license" means an authorization that permits the holder to engage in the practice of a profession regulated under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301.5(2): (4); (6) Subject to Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-301.5(2)(a): the commission determines that the license issued by the other state, district, or territory encompasses a similar scope of practice as the license sought in this state;

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-302 Term of license -- Expiration -- Renewal.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-302(1): The commission shall issue each license under this chapter in accordance with a renewal cycle established by rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-302(2): At the time of renewal, the licensee shall show satisfactory evidence of compliance with renewal requirements established by rule by the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-302(3): Each license automatically expires on the expiration date shown on the license unless the licensee renews it in accordance with the rules established by the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303 Grounds for denial of license -- Disciplinary proceedings -- Reinstatement.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(1): The commission shall refuse to issue a license to an applicant and shall refuse to renew or shall revoke, suspend, restrict, place on probation, or otherwise act upon the license of a licensee who does not meet the qualifications for licensure under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(2): The commission may refuse to issue a license to an applicant and may refuse to renew or may revoke, suspend, restrict, place on probation, issue a public or private reprimand to, or otherwise act upon the license of any licensee if:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(2)(a): the applicant or licensee has engaged in unlawful or unprofessional conduct, as defined by statute or rule under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(2)(b): the applicant or licensee has been determined to be mentally incompetent for any reason by a court of competent jurisdiction; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(2)(c): the applicant or licensee is unable to practice the occupation or profession with reasonable skill and safety because of illness, drunkenness, excessive use of drugs, narcotics, chemicals, or any other type of material, or as a result of any other mental or physical condition, when the licensee's condition demonstrates a threat or potential threat to the public health, safety, or welfare, as determined by a ringside physician or the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(3): Any licensee whose license under this chapter has been suspended, revoked, or restricted may apply for reinstatement of the license at reasonable intervals and upon compliance with any conditions imposed upon the licensee by statute, rule, or terms of the license suspension, revocation, or restriction.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(4): (1); (2) The commission may issue cease and desist orders:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(4)(a): (1); (2) to a licensee or applicant who may be disciplined under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(4)(b): to any person who otherwise violates this chapter or any rules adopted under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(5): (5); Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act; (5)
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(5)(a): The commission may impose an administrative fine for acts of unprofessional or unlawful conduct under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(5)(b): (5) An administrative fine under this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(5)(c): Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act The commission shall comply with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(5)(d): (5) The imposition of a fine under this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(6): (6)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(6)(a): (6)(b) The commission may not take disciplinary action against any person for unlawful or unprofessional conduct under this chapter, unless the commission initiates an adjudicative proceeding regarding the conduct within four years after the conduct is reported to the commission, except under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(6)(b): The commission may not take disciplinary action against any person for unlawful or unprofessional conduct more than 10 years after the occurrence of the conduct, unless the proceeding is in response to a civil or criminal judgment or settlement and the proceeding is initiated within one year following the judgment or settlement.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-303(7): Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304 Additional fees for promoter -- Dedicated credits -- Promotion of contests -- Annual exemption of showcase event.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(1): In addition to the payment of any other fees and money due under this chapter, a promoter shall pay a license fee and, if applicable, a broadcast revenue fee determined by the commission and established in rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(2): Fees collected by the commission under this section shall be retained by the commission as a dedicated credit to be used by the commission to award grants to organizations that promote amateur boxing in the state and cover commission expenses.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(3): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (2); (2) In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(3)(a): (2) governing the manner in which applications for grants under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(a): For the purpose of creating a greater interest in contests in the state, the commission may exempt from the payment of license fees under this section one contest or exhibition in each calendar year, intended as a showcase event.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(b): The commission shall select the contest or exhibition to be exempted based on factors which include:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(b)(i): attraction of the optimum number of spectators;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(b)(ii): costs of promoting and producing the contest or exhibition;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(b)(iii): ticket pricing;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(b)(iv): committed promotions and advertising of the contest or exhibition;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(b)(v): rankings and quality of the contestants; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-304(4)(b)(vi): committed television and other media coverage of the contest or exhibition.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309 Medical examinations and drug tests.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The commission shall adopt rules in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(1)(a): produce evidence based upon competent laboratory examination that they are HIV negative as a condition of participating as a contestant in any contest;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(1)(b): be subject to random drug testing before or after participation in a contest, and sanctions, including barring participation in a contest or withholding a percentage of any purse, that shall be placed against a contestant testing positive for alcohol or any other drug that in the opinion of the commission is inconsistent with the safe and competent participation of that contestant in a contest;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(1)(c): be subject to a medical examination by the ringside physician not more than 30 hours before the contest to identify any physical ailment or communicable disease that, in the opinion of the commission or designated commission member, are inconsistent with the safe and competent participation of that contestant in the contest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(1)(d): be subject to medical testing for communicable diseases as considered necessary by the commission to protect the health, safety, and welfare of the licensees and the public.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(2)(a): Medical information concerning a contestant shall be provided by the contestant or medical professional or laboratory.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-309(2)(b): A promoter or manager may not provide to or receive from the commission medical information concerning a contestant.

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311 Ringside physician.
--------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(1): (2) The commission shall maintain a list of ringside physicians who hold a Doctor of Medicine (MD) degree and are registered with the commission as approved to act as a ringside physician and meet the requirements of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(2)(a): The commission shall appoint a registered ringside physician to perform the duties of a ringside physician at each contest held under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(2)(b): The promoter of a contest shall pay a fee determined by the commission by rule to the commission for a ringside physician.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(3): An applicant for registration as a ringside physician shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(3)(a): submit an application for registration;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(3)(b): provide the commission with evidence of the applicant's licensure to practice medicine in the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(3)(c): satisfy minimum qualifications established by the department by rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(4): A ringside physician at attendance at a contest:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(4)(a): may stop the contest at any point if the ringside physician determines that a contestant's physical condition renders the contestant unable to safely continue the contest; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-311(4)(b): works under the direction of the commission.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-312 Contracts.
-----------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-312(1): Before a contest is held, a copy of the signed contract or agreement between the promoter of the contest and each contestant shall be filed with the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-312(2): Approval of the contract's terms and conditions shall be obtained from the commission as a condition precedent to the contest.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-313 Withholding of purse.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-313(1): The commission, the director, or any other agent authorized by the commission may order a promoter to withhold any part of a purse or other money belonging or payable to any contestant, manager, or second if, in the judgment of the commission, director, or other agent:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-313(1)(a): the contestant is not competing honestly or to the best of the contestant's skill and ability or the contestant otherwise violates any rules adopted by the commission or any of the provisions of this chapter; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-313(1)(b): the manager or second violates any rules adopted by the commission or any of the provisions of this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-313(2): This section does not apply to any contestant in a wrestling exhibition who appears not to be competing honestly or to the best of the contestant's skill and ability.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-313(3): Upon the withholding of any part of a purse or other money pursuant to this section, the commission shall immediately schedule a hearing on the matter, provide adequate notice to all interested parties, and dispose of the matter as promptly as possible.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-313(4): If it is determined that a contestant, manager, or second is not entitled to any part of that person's share of the purse or other money, the promoter shall pay the money over to the commission.

------------------------------------------------------------
A person who engages in any act of unlawful conduct, as defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-315 Exemptions.
------------------------------------------
This chapter does not apply to:Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-315(1): (1)(a); (b) any amateur contest or exhibition of unarmed combat conducted by or participated in exclusively by:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-315(1)(a): a school accredited by the Board of Education;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-315(1)(b): a college or university accredited by the United States Department of Education; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-315(1)(c): (1)(a); (b) any association or organization of a school, college, or university described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-315(2): any contest or exhibition of unarmed combat conducted in accordance with the standards and regulations of USA Boxing, Inc.; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-315(3): a white-collar contest.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316 Contest weights and classes -- Matching contestants.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The commission shall make rules in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(2): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The commission shall make rules in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(3): (3)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(3)(a): As to any unarmed combat contest, a contestant may not fight another contestant who is outside of the contestant's weight classification.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(3)(b): (3)(a) Notwithstanding Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(4): (3)(b) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(4)(a): a contestant who has contracted to participate in a given weight class may not be permitted to compete if the contestant is not within that weight class at the weigh-in; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(4)(b): a contestant may have two hours to attempt to gain or lose not more than three pounds in order to be reweighed.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5)(a): As to any unarmed combat contest, the commission may not allow a contest in which the contestants are not fairly matched.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5)(b): Factors in determining if contestants are fairly matched include:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5)(b)(i): the win-loss record of the contestants;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5)(b)(ii): the weight differential between the contestants;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5)(b)(iii): the caliber of opponents for each contestant;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5)(b)(iv): each contestant's number of fights; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-316(5)(b)(v): previous suspensions or disciplinary actions of the contestants.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317 Elimination contests -- Conduct of contests -- Applicability of provisions -- Limitations on license -- Duration of contests -- Equipment -- Limitations on contests.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(1): An elimination unarmed combat contest shall be conducted under the supervision and authority of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(2): Except as otherwise provided in this section and except as otherwise provided by specific statute, the provisions of this chapter pertaining to boxing apply to an elimination unarmed combat contest.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(3)(a): All contests in an elimination unarmed combat contest shall be no more than three rounds in duration.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(3)(b): A round of unarmed combat in an elimination unarmed combat contest shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(3)(b)(i): be no more than one minute in duration; or
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(3)(b)(ii): be up to three minutes in duration if there is only a single round.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(3)(c): A period of rest following a round shall be no more than one minute in duration.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(4): A contestant:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(4)(a): shall wear gloves approved by the commission; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(4)(b): shall wear headgear approved by the commission, the designated commission member, or the director if a designated commission member is not present.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-317(5): A contestant may participate in more than one contest, but may not participate in more than a total of seven rounds in the entire tournament.


Utah Code Annotated § 9-23-318 Commission rulemaking.
-----------------------------------------------------
The commission may make rules governing the conduct of a contest held under this chapter to protect the health and safety of licensees and members of the public.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 9 - Chapter 24 - Utah Main Street Program Act
*************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-101 Definitions.
-------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-101(1): "Center" means the National Main Street Center.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-101(2): 9-24-102 "Program" means the Utah Main Street Program created in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102 Utah Main Street Program.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(1): The Utah Main Street Program is created within the department to provide resources for the revitalization of downtown or commercial district areas of municipalities in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(2): To implement the program, the department may:
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(2)(a): become a member of the National Main Street Center and partner with the center to become the statewide coordinating program for participating municipalities in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(2)(b): establish criteria for the designation of one or more local main street programs administered by a county or municipality in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(2)(c): provide training and technical assistance to local governments, businesses, property owners, or other organizations that participate in designated local main street programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(2)(d): subject to appropriations from the Legislature or other funding, provide financial assistance to designated local main street programs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(2)(e): under the direction of the executive director, appoint full-time staff.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(3): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(3)(a): local government support of the local main street program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(3)(b): collecting data to measure economic development impact.
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(4): 9-1-208 The department shall include in the annual written report described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(4)(a): a local main street program designation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 9-24-102(4)(b): financial support from the program.
